<script>
    $(document).ready(function(){
        var timeout;

		$('.block-suggester-container').on('click',function(e){

			e.stopPropagation();

        });

        $('.block-suggester-container .suggester input[type=text]').keyup(function(){
            var self = $(this);

            if(timeout) clearTimeout(timeout);

            timeout = setTimeout(function(){
                $.nette.ajax({
                    url: "https:\/\/www.kosik.cz\/vanoce\/darky?do=suggester-suggest",
                    data: {
                        phrase: self.val()
                    }
                })
            }, 300);


        });

    });

    function gaPush(self, cat)
    {
        dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'ga.pageview',
            'pagePath': '/hledat?q='+$('#frm-suggester-suggester-phrase').val()+'&cat='+cat,
            'pageTitle': 'Našeptávač'
        });

        window.location = self.href;
    }
</script>

        <input type="hidden" name="do" value="suggester-suggester-submit"><!--[if IE]><input type=IEbug disabled style="display:none"><![endif]-->
</form>

    </div>

    var ShoppingList = {

        var textArea = document.getElementById('frm-shoppingList-listForm-queries');

            textArea.setAttribute('placeholder', 'Například: \n\nMléko \nChléb \nVejce \nMaso \nRajče \n\n\nPro zadání klikněte do pole')
    });

</script>

        <script>
            $(document).ready(function () {
                $('.region-navigation ul > li.sub').hover(function () {
                    var isOpen = $(this).data().open;

                    if (!isOpen) {
                        var images = $(this).find('img');

                        images.each(function (index, element) {
                            $(element).attr('src', $(element).data().src);
                        });

                        $(this).data().open = true;
                    }
                });
            });
        </script>

        $('.christmas-link').on('click', function () {
            if (window.innerWidth < 1025) {
                var mobileMenu = $('#big-menu');
                mobileMenu.toggleClass('open');
                basic.toggleClass((document.querySelector('body')), 'open-menu');

<script type="text/javascript" id="snippet-productFilter-scriptArea">
	$('.filter-more-result-column').hide();

//    $(document).ready(function () {
        $(document).ajaxComplete(function() {

            $('.filter-ajax-waiting').removeClass('show');


            var brandClass = 'show';
            var formRowClass = 'form-row';
            var filterCategoriesClass = 'filter-categories';
            var buttonsShowMoreClass = 'show-more-brands';
            var buttonsShowLessClass = 'show-less-brands';
            var filters = $('.filter-more-result');
            var defaultFilterInputs = {"brand":[87,1877,3267,55,670,3374,3567,3319,2356,3441]};

            function hideCheckboxes(rows, key) {

                if (rows.legnth <= 10) {
                    return;
                }

            rows.each(function (i, e) {
                var val = +$(e).find("input").val();
                var arr = defaultFilterInputs[key];

                if ($.inArray(val, arr) === -1) {
                    $(e).hide();
                }
            });
        }

            $('.' + buttonsShowMoreClass).on('click', function (e) {
                e.stopPropagation();

                var filterCategories = $(this).closest('.' + filterCategoriesClass);

                for (var key in defaultFilterInputs) {
                    if (defaultFilterInputs.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
                        if (filterCategories.attr("id") === "filter-" + key) {
                            continue;
                        }
                        var rows = $('#filter-' + key + ' .' + formRowClass);
                        hideCheckboxes(rows, key);
                        $('#filter-' + key + ' .' + buttonsShowMoreClass).show();
                    }
                }

                filterCategories
                        .find('.' + formRowClass)
                        .show();

                $('.' + buttonsShowLessClass).hide();

                filterCategories
                        .find('.' + buttonsShowLessClass)
                        .show();

                $(this).hide();
            });


            $('.' + buttonsShowLessClass).on('click', function (e) {
                e.stopPropagation();

                var filterCategories = $(this).closest('.' + filterCategoriesClass);
                var key = filterCategories.attr("id").split("-")[1];
                var rows = filterCategories.find('.' + formRowClass);

                hideCheckboxes(rows, key);

                filterCategories
                        .find('.' + buttonsShowMoreClass)
                        .show();

                $(this).hide();
            });

            filters.on('click', function(e){
                e.stopPropagation();
            });

            $('html, body').on('click', function(){
                filters.removeClass(brandClass);
            });

            $('.filter-more-result .kosik-modal-close').on('click', function () {
                filters.removeClass(brandClass);
            });

            $('.filter-constraint').each(function () {
                enableAutoSubmit('#' + $(this).attr('id'));
            });

            function enableAutoSubmit(selector) {

                if ($(selector).hasClass('filter-range')) {
                    $(document).on('mouseup', selector, function () {
                        $('.filter-ajax-waiting').addClass('show');
                        $(this).closest('form').submit();
                    });
                }

//                $(document).ajaxComplete(function(){
//                    $('.filter-ajax-waiting').removeClass('show');
//                })
            }
        });
//    });
</script>

    var onProductModalDestroy = function() {

    	var pageData = window.dataLayer[0];

        pageData["event"] = "ga.pageview";
        pageData["pagePath"] = window.location.pathname;
        pageData["pageTitle"] = window.document.title;

	    dataLayer.push(pageData);
    };
</script>

    	var pageData = window.dataLayer[0];

<script async>
    basic.documentReady(function () {
        $.get("\/vanoce\/darky?do=productList-ajaxLoaderSetting").done(function (setting) {
            setting.ShowButton = false;
            ajaxLoader.init(setting);
        });
    });

    var onProductModalDestroy = function() {

    	var pageData = window.dataLayer[0];

        pageData["event"] = "ga.pageview";
        pageData["pagePath"] = window.location.pathname;
        pageData["pageTitle"] = window.document.title;

	    dataLayer.push(pageData);
    };
</script>
